I have a weird auditory problem some pitches and sounds will make me feel nauseated and light-headed. I can't tolerate certain lower pitches in women that are often heard in gospel, country, and certain types of jazz (a huge disappointment to my jazz-loving father.) I have never noticed that issue when siblings or children and parents are singing together.  I find these two so calming.
